Turn to Self

Find your
still
point.

Our ego is often depicted as the black sheep of the human experience, which can be true when our ego is in charge and we live a hedonistic and selfish life but here we say that, the same ego, infused and blended with the qualities of our soul, can serve us to create a life founded in compassion, empathy and all other qualities that define a conscious human being.

In our aspiration to paint our individual ego with the colors of the human soul, here is our playbook.

Everything we write about, everything you will learn is only on a conceptual level. Until you experience them in real life events and situations, their transformative effects on you and your personality will be very minimal, but we have to start somewhere.

Accepting what is and isn't.

However you move through your inner world — whether that's sitting in silence, chanting, praying, dancing, creating art, meditating or simply not knowing yet — this is half of the work. The remaining half is how we internalize the situations and the events in our lives and furthermore, how we are able to deal with them.

Our only aim is to make you come to the awareness and to realize that all you need, everything you need to heal whatever needs healing — be it emotional, physical, mental, psychological — the answers, the solutions, all of them are within you, inside of you. All we need is the guidance to reach the endless wisdom within us. This is why all our exercises are directed to guide your focus inward, where you will reach all the answers you are seeking. This is the main reason why we are relentless against any situation that could impair or cause you to deviate your focus from turning inward.
Start here

Offerings

01

Meditation
Groups

→

Here the first step and our most powerful tool for this is our attention and our focus. Once we are able to maintain our focus and sit down for our meditation, we also need to work on "letting go" and "not trying" in order to help ourselves to fall into a natural meditative state.

But how does one get to the meditative state? Not so easy, is it? Anyone can teach you how to meditate, there are numerous techniques but no one can actually make you meditate.

Neither can we but we know one thing: how to cultivate the mind and the body for it to awaken this energy that is already inside of you and once it is awakened, we connect to it to begin our inner journey.

We are creating groups that are ideally between 8 to 9 people. Each group will have one leader and one aid.

For the ones who have devoted themselves to full-time Meditation, the physical gatherings at their center will be twice a day, during dawn and dusk.

At the minimum, each group leader will organize at least one physical meditation gathering per week.
02

Live
Q&A

→

Monthly Q&A sessions on Self Realization, and how to integrate this into our lives. A space for honest questions — an inquiry into what is unfolding within us and how to deal with it.

03

Private
Consultation

→

One-on-one time with Cem. A private space to share your inner journey, ask what you cannot ask in a group, and receive guidance specific to where you are on your path.

04

Silent
Retreats

→

To support the inner awakening, we further cultivate the path through monthly mini silent retreats. Each month, during the full moon, we will meet at one of the group leader's or members' homes, or at the meditation center, to practice silence and stillness. This could range from two to three days per month.
05

Nature
Outings

→

Apart from the meditations, we will also spend time in nature — gathering early in the morning to watch the sunrise and the sunset at dusk, sometimes followed by a short walk with some light yoga. We will arrange outings in nature: the forest, the beach, anywhere we can connect to nature.

Rules & Dynamics

How we
walk
together.

Rules

This is not a social group, we are gathered here for each of us to walk on our own path. Sharing your own journey with others is not advised, if you have to, then you can, with your leader and only with them.

We welcome your "presence", your "silence and stillness". This is not an intellectual spirituality platform.

No "answer questions" (meaning; questions where you yourself are answering your own questions).

Members can of course socialize between themselves on their own time but not during group events.

We will also have monthly Q&A sessions on Self Realization. Keep in mind: talking prior to "Self Realization" only adds confusion for all! "Save yourself first"

How we walk
each other
home.

Dynamics

The aim of all the activities is to support each other's inner world. Achieving a more balanced and calm inner state will help all of us in dealing with the demands of the outer world. We all still need to fine-tune our inner skills when facing challenging events in our lives.

We all end up wearing a mask, be it of a spouse, a mother, a father, a son, a daughter, a sibling, a boss, an employee and many many more. We rarely can be our true self. Sometimes we are not even aware that we have a mask on. This is a space, where you can lay down all your masks and be yourself. A way to find out who we truly are beyond that social identity.

In facing ourselves, we can get in touch both with the darkness & the light within us, as we do our inner work. By realizing our essence and resting there, in time and with practice we are able to face our triggers and learn how to see and feel through them, which will all dissolve in front of us.

The inner work will also guide us towards seeing and feeling our calling & start working and living the life of our true purpose.

When our teacher works for hours with endless motivation for our group, we sometimes ask him where he finds the energy to do all this work. He tells us that, "when they look at me from the outside, to them, what I'm doing might look like work, but for me, since I love what I am doing, I don't see it as work and instead of it draining me, it energizes me."

Our aim for all is to find what they love so that they will never feel drained or tired from what they do but always feel energized and uplifted and making what you love your work, as it is often said, "do what you love and you'll never work a day in your life" — and let your service serve you and others to create a life that is both meaningful and fulfilling.

Giving your time to any part of this will help heal, at least to some extent, almost all chronic diseases, be it physical, mental, or emotional.

There are times when we will need to face some of our challenges alone but we don't have to build or prepare ourselves alone. Each one of us in our group is here for each other to help one another on our journey.

A note

Wherever Cem is traveling, whichever town or city he is at, it is free to join to meditate. All you need to do is bring yourself.

It is also free to join the silent retreats (if there is space available) but you do pay or bring your own food.

What we charge for:
— Helping you create your Meditation Group.
— Private Silence and Stillness Retreats.
— Private Consultations.

The Ultimate GiftOnce awakened no one day will ever be the same as another. Every day is a new day not because we're doing new things or visiting a different geography, the same things the same people the same books will all mean or relate to us in different ways.

So it is you creating a new, different day because of the changes within you, versus seeking this externally.

The same goes for daily meditation and any exercise that facilitates turning in.

Also with being alone and staying alone, which becomes very entertaining than anything transpiring on the outside.

This is a journey, learning through the teachings here and through your interactions with others, you will have some direct experiences, which all carry value. Although these all can be useful on your path, truth is a secret and is not directly disclosed.

Some will be satisfied following the crowds, a few will choose to follow their hearts and will receive their answers when it is their time.
